# build.ps1
$vsPath = "C:\Program Files (x86)\Microsoft Visual Studio\2022\BuildTools"
$vsDevShell = "$vsPath\Common7\Tools\Launch-VsDevShell.ps1"

if (Test-Path $vsDevShell) {
    Write-Host "Initializing VS Developer Shell..."
    & $vsDevShell -Arch amd64 -HostArch amd64 -SkipAutomaticLocation

    # Create build directory if it doesn't exist, or clean it if possible
    if (!(Test-Path "build")) {
        New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path "build"
    } else {
        Write-Host "Build directory exists. Attempting to clean..."
        try {
            Get-ChildItem -Path "build" -Recurse | Remove-Item -Force -Recurse -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
        } catch {
            Write-Warning "Could not fully clean build directory. Continuing with existing directory."
        }
    }

    # Change to the src-interceptor directory for message compilation
    Push-Location "src-interceptor"

    Write-Host "Skipping message compilation for now..."
    <# Temporarily commented out message compilation
    # Compile message resources
    Write-Host "Compiling message resources..."
    $mcPath = "${env:WindowsSdkDir}bin\${env:WindowsSDKVersion}x64\mc.exe"
    $rcPath = "${env:WindowsSdkDir}bin\${env:WindowsSDKVersion}x64\rc.exe"

    if (!(Test-Path $mcPath)) {
        Write-Host "Message Compiler not found at $mcPath"
        Write-Host "Checking alternate locations..."
        $mcPath = (Get-Command mc.exe -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue).Source
        if (!$mcPath) {
            Write-Error "Message Compiler (mc.exe) not found. Please ensure Windows SDK is installed."
            exit 1
        }
    }

    if (!(Test-Path $rcPath)) {
        Write-Host "Resource Compiler not found at $rcPath"
        Write-Host "Checking alternate locations..."
        $rcPath = (Get-Command rc.exe -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue).Source
        if (!$rcPath) {
            Write-Error "Resource Compiler (rc.exe) not found. Please ensure Windows SDK is installed."
            exit 1
        }
    }

    Write-Host "Using Message Compiler: $mcPath"
    Write-Host "Using Resource Compiler: $rcPath"

    # Compile the message file
    & $mcPath -U PrinterInterceptor.mc
    if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
        Write-Error "Message compilation failed"
        exit 1
    }

    # Compile the resource file
    & $rcPath PrinterInterceptor.rc
    if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
        Write-Error "Resource compilation failed"
        exit 1
    }
    #>

    # Return to root directory
    Pop-Location

    # Configure CMake
    Write-Host "Configuring CMake..."
    cmake -B build -A x64
    if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
        Write-Error "CMake configuration failed"
        exit 1
    }

    # Build the project
    Write-Host "Building..."
    cmake --build build --config Release
    if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {
        Write-Error "Build failed"
        exit 1
    }

    Write-Host "Build completed successfully"
} else {
    Write-Error "Could not find VS Developer Shell at: $vsDevShell"
}

# File: C:\Users\Slyphur\Documents\interceptor\install.ps1

Write-Host "Checking Print Spooler service..."
Get-PrinterPort

# Stop the spooler service
Write-Host "Stopping Print Spooler service..."
Stop-Service -Name "Spooler" -Force

# Create the destination directory if it doesn't exist
$dllPath = "$env:SystemRoot\System32"
if (!(Test-Path $dllPath)) {
    New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $dllPath -Force
}

# Copy the DLL to System32
Write-Host "Copying DLL to System32..."
Copy-Item "build\Release\PrinterInterceptor.dll" -Destination "$dllPath\PrinterInterceptor.dll" -Force

# Import the registry entries
Write-Host "Installing registry entries..."
reg import "install.reg"

# Start the spooler service
Write-Host "Starting Print Spooler service..."
Start-Service -Name "Spooler"

Write-Host "Checking Print Spooler service..."
Get-PrinterPort

# Start the interceptor threads by calling the exported function from the DLL
Write-Host "Starting interceptor threads..."
$attempts = 0
$maxAttempts = 3
$success = $false

# Kill any existing rundll32 processes that might be running our DLL
Write-Host "Stopping any existing PrinterInterceptor processes..."
Get-Process rundll32 -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue | Where-Object { $_.CommandLine -like '*PrinterInterceptor*' } | Stop-Process -Force

# Wait a moment for processes to clean up
Start-Sleep -Seconds 2

while ($attempts -lt $maxAttempts -and -not $success) {
    try {
        $attempts++
        Write-Host "`nAttempt $attempts to start interceptor threads..."
        
        # Try to start the threads with full path and elevated privileges
        $startInfo = New-Object System.Diagnostics.ProcessStartInfo
        $startInfo.FileName = "rundll32.exe"
        $startInfo.Arguments = "`"$env:SystemRoot\System32\PrinterInterceptor.dll`",StartInterceptorThreads"
        $startInfo.UseShellExecute = $true
        $startInfo.Verb = "runas"
        $startInfo.RedirectStandardOutput = $false
        $startInfo.RedirectStandardError = $false
        $startInfo.WindowStyle = 'Hidden'
        
        Write-Host "Starting process: $($startInfo.FileName) $($startInfo.Arguments)"
        $process = [System.Diagnostics.Process]::Start($startInfo)
        
        # Wait for the process to start
        Start-Sleep -Seconds 3
        
        # Check if the pipe exists
        Write-Host "Checking for named pipes..."
        $pipes = [System.IO.Directory]::GetFiles("\\.\\pipe\\")
        $interceptorPipe = $pipes | Where-Object { $_ -like "*PrinterInterceptorPortPipe*" }
        
        if ($interceptorPipe) {
            $success = $true
            Write-Host "Interceptor threads started successfully!"
            Write-Host "Found pipe: $interceptorPipe"
        } else {
            Write-Host "Available pipes:"
            $pipes | ForEach-Object { Write-Host "  $_" }
            Write-Host "PrinterInterceptor pipe not found, threads may not have started properly."
            
            # Check if the DLL exists and is accessible
            if (Test-Path "$env:SystemRoot\System32\PrinterInterceptor.dll") {
                Write-Host "DLL exists in System32"
                $dllInfo = Get-Item "$env:SystemRoot\System32\PrinterInterceptor.dll"
                Write-Host "DLL Details:"
                Write-Host "  Last Write Time: $($dllInfo.LastWriteTime)"
                Write-Host "  Size: $($dllInfo.Length) bytes"
            } else {
                Write-Host "ERROR: DLL not found in System32!"
            }
            
            # Check registry
            Write-Host "Checking registry..."
            $regPath = "HKLM:\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Print\Monitors\PrinterInterceptor"
            if (Test-Path $regPath) {
                Write-Host "Registry key exists"
                Get-ItemProperty $regPath | Format-List
            } else {
                Write-Host "ERROR: Registry key not found!"
            }
            
            if ($attempts -lt $maxAttempts) {
                Write-Host "Waiting before retry..."
                Start-Sleep -Seconds 5
            }
        }
    } catch {
        Write-Host "Error starting threads: $_"
        Write-Host $_.Exception.Message
        Write-Host $_.Exception.StackTrace
        if ($attempts -lt $maxAttempts) {
            Write-Host "Waiting before retry..."
            Start-Sleep -Seconds 5
        }
    }
}

if (-not $success) {
    Write-Host "`nWARNING: Could not verify if interceptor threads started properly."
    Write-Host "Please check the following:"
    Write-Host "1. Verify PrinterInterceptor.dll exists in $env:SystemRoot\System32"
    Write-Host "2. Check if the DLL is properly registered in the registry"
    Write-Host "3. Make sure you're running with administrator privileges"
    Write-Host "4. Check Event Viewer for any error messages"
    Write-Host "`nTry running this command manually:"
    Write-Host "rundll32.exe $env:SystemRoot\System32\PrinterInterceptor.dll,StartInterceptorThreads"
} else {
    Write-Host "`nInstallation complete. The port monitor is now installed and running."
}

Write-Host "`nYou can now add a printer using one of these ports:"
Write-Host "- SplitPrinterInterceptor"

# File: C:\Users\Slyphur\Documents\interceptor\PrinterInterceptor.cpp

#include <strsafe.h>
#include <sddl.h>

#define PIPE_NAME L"\\\\.\\pipe\\PrinterInterceptor"
#define PORT_COMMAND_PIPE L"\\\\.\\pipe\\PrinterInterceptorPort"

// Add message resource definitions
#define MSG_PIPE_CREATE_ATTEMPT 0x1
#define MSG_PIPE_CREATE_SUCCESS 0x2
#define MSG_PIPE_CREATE_FAILURE 0x3
#define MSG_PIPE_ACCESS_ERROR   0x4

void WriteToEventLog(LPCWSTR message, LPCWSTR additionalInfo = nullptr) {
    // Write to debug output for debugging
    OutputDebugStringW(message);
    if (additionalInfo) {
        OutputDebugStringW(L": ");
        OutputDebugStringW(additionalInfo);
    }
    OutputDebugStringW(L"\n");

    // Open the event log
    HANDLE hEventLog = RegisterEventSourceW(NULL, L"PrinterInterceptor");
    if (hEventLog) {
        // Prepare the strings array
        LPCWSTR strings[2] = { message, additionalInfo };
        WORD numStrings = additionalInfo ? 2 : 1;

        // Report the event
        ReportEventW(
            hEventLog,                   // Event log handle
            EVENTLOG_INFORMATION_TYPE,   // Event type
            0,                          // Category (unused)
            MSG_PIPE_CREATE_ATTEMPT,    // Event ID
            NULL,                       // User SID (unused)
            numStrings,                 // Number of strings
            0,                          // Size of raw data
            strings,                    // String array
            NULL                        // Raw data
        );

        DeregisterEventSource(hEventLog);
    }

    // Write to file for persistent logging
    try {
        SYSTEMTIME st;
        GetLocalTime(&st);
        
        wchar_t timestamp[100];
        swprintf_s(timestamp, L"[%04d-%02d-%02d %02d:%02d:%02d.%03d] ",
            st.wYear, st.wMonth, st.wDay,
            st.wHour, st.wMinute, st.wSecond, st.wMilliseconds);

        // Create directory if it doesn't exist
        CreateDirectoryW(L"C:\\PrinterLogs", NULL);

        // Open file in append mode
        HANDLE hFile = CreateFileW(
            L"C:\\PrinterLogs\\interceptor.log",
            FILE_APPEND_DATA,
            FILE_SHARE_READ,
            NULL,
            OPEN_ALWAYS,
            FILE_ATTRIBUTE_NORMAL,
            NULL
        );

        if (hFile != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            // Write timestamp
            DWORD written;
            WriteFile(hFile, timestamp, (DWORD)(wcslen(timestamp) * sizeof(WCHAR)), &written, NULL);
            
            // Write message
            WriteFile(hFile, message, (DWORD)(wcslen(message) * sizeof(WCHAR)), &written, NULL);
            
            // Write additional info if present
            if (additionalInfo) {
                WriteFile(hFile, L": ", 2 * sizeof(WCHAR), &written, NULL);
                WriteFile(hFile, additionalInfo, (DWORD)(wcslen(additionalInfo) * sizeof(WCHAR)), &written, NULL);
            }
            
            // Write newline
            WriteFile(hFile, L"\r\n", 2 * sizeof(WCHAR), &written, NULL);
            
            CloseHandle(hFile);
        }
    }
    catch (...) {
        // Ignore any errors during file writing
    }
}

HANDLE CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(LPCWSTR pipeName, DWORD openMode, DWORD pipeMode, PSECURITY_ATTRIBUTES pSA) {
    char logBuffer[512];
    sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Creating pipe '%ws' with openMode=0x%x, pipeMode=0x%x\n", pipeName, openMode, pipeMode);
    WriteToEventLog(logBuffer);

    // Create a security descriptor that allows everyone to access the pipe
    SECURITY_DESCRIPTOR sd;
    SECURITY_ATTRIBUTES sa;
    if (!InitializeSecurityDescriptor(&sd, SECURITY_DESCRIPTOR_REVISION)) {
        DWORD error = GetLastError();
        sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Failed to initialize security descriptor for pipe '%ws', error=0x%x (%d)\n", 
                 pipeName, error, error);
        WriteToEventLog(logBuffer);
        return INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }

    // Set the DACL to NULL for full access to everyone
    if (!SetSecurityDescriptorDacl(&sd, TRUE, NULL, FALSE)) {
        DWORD error = GetLastError();
        sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Failed to set security descriptor DACL for pipe '%ws', error=0x%x (%d)\n", 
                 pipeName, error, error);
        WriteToEventLog(logBuffer);
        return INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }

    sa.nLength = sizeof(SECURITY_ATTRIBUTES);
    sa.lpSecurityDescriptor = &sd;
    sa.bInheritHandle = FALSE;

    HANDLE hPipe = CreateNamedPipeW(
        pipeName,
        openMode,
        pipeMode,
        1,
        4096,
        4096,
        0,
        &sa
    );

    if (hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        DWORD error = GetLastError();
        sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Failed to create pipe '%ws', error=0x%x (%d)\n", pipeName, error, error);
        WriteToEventLog(logBuffer);
        return INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }

    sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Successfully created pipe '%ws', handle=0x%p\n", pipeName, hPipe);
    WriteToEventLog(logBuffer);

    // Verify the pipe is accessible
    HANDLE hTest = CreateFileW(
        pipeName,
        GENERIC_READ | GENERIC_WRITE,
        0,
        NULL,
        OPEN_EXISTING,
        0,
        NULL
    );

    if (hTest == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        DWORD error = GetLastError();
        if (error == ERROR_PIPE_BUSY) {
            sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Pipe '%ws' exists but is busy\n", pipeName);
        } else {
            sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Pipe '%ws' exists but is not accessible, error=0x%x (%d)\n", pipeName, error, error);
        }
        WriteToEventLog(logBuffer);
    } else {
        CloseHandle(hTest);
        sprintf_s(logBuffer, "PipeServerThread: Pipe '%ws' is accessible\n", pipeName);
        WriteToEventLog(logBuffer);
    }

    return hPipe;
}

DWORD WINAPI PipeServerThread(LPVOID lpParam) {
    WriteToLog("PipeServerThread: Starting...");
    
    while (true) {
        WriteToLog("PipeServerThread: Creating new pipe instance...");
        
        DWORD openMode = PIPE_ACCESS_INBOUND;
        DWORD pipeMode = PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT;
        
        char logBuffer[512];
        sprintf_s(logBuffer, sizeof(logBuffer), "PipeServerThread: Creating pipe with openMode=0x%X, pipeMode=0x%X", 
                 openMode, pipeMode);
        WriteToLog(logBuffer);

        HANDLE hPipe = CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(PIPE_NAME, openMode, pipeMode, NULL);
        
        if (hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            WriteToLog("PipeServerThread: Failed to create pipe after all retries. Thread exiting.");
            return 1;
        }

        WriteToLog("PipeServerThread: Waiting for client connection...");
        
        BOOL connected = ConnectNamedPipe(hPipe, NULL);
        if (!connected) {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            sprintf_s(logBuffer, sizeof(logBuffer), "PipeServerThread: ConnectNamedPipe failed. Error: %lu (0x%08X)", 
                     error, error);
            WriteToLog(logBuffer);
            CloseHandle(hPipe);
            continue;
        }

        WriteToLog("PipeServerThread: Client connected. Reading data...");
        
        // ... rest of the existing pipe handling code ...
    }
    return 0;
}

DWORD WINAPI PortConfigThread(LPVOID lpParam) {
    WriteToLog("PortConfigThread: Starting...");
    
    while (true) {
        WriteToLog("PortConfigThread: Creating new pipe instance...");
        
        DWORD openMode = PIPE_ACCESS_INBOUND;
        DWORD pipeMode = PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT;
        
        char logBuffer[512];
        sprintf_s(logBuffer, sizeof(logBuffer), "PortConfigThread: Creating pipe with openMode=0x%X, pipeMode=0x%X", 
                 openMode, pipeMode);
        WriteToLog(logBuffer);

        HANDLE hPipe = CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(PORT_COMMAND_PIPE, openMode, pipeMode, NULL);
        
        if (hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            WriteToLog("PortConfigThread: Failed to create pipe after all retries. Thread exiting.");
            return 1;
        }

        WriteToLog("PortConfigThread: Waiting for client connection...");
        
        BOOL connected = ConnectNamedPipe(hPipe, NULL);
        if (!connected) {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            sprintf_s(logBuffer, sizeof(logBuffer), "PortConfigThread: ConnectNamedPipe failed. Error: %lu (0x%08X)", 
                     error, error);
            WriteToLog(logBuffer);
            CloseHandle(hPipe);
            continue;
        }

        WriteToLog("PortConfigThread: Client connected. Reading data...");
        
        // ... rest of the existing pipe handling code ...
    }
    return 0;
}

BOOL APIENTRY DllMain(HMODULE hModule, DWORD ul_reason_for_call, LPVOID lpReserved) {
    switch (ul_reason_for_call) {
        case DLL_PROCESS_ATTACH: {
            // Register event source with message file
            HKEY hKey;
            DWORD disposition;
            if (RegCreateKeyExW(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE,
                L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Services\\EventLog\\Application\\PrinterInterceptor",
                0, NULL, REG_OPTION_NON_VOLATILE, KEY_SET_VALUE, NULL, &hKey, &disposition) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                
                wchar_t path[MAX_PATH];
                GetModuleFileNameW(hModule, path, MAX_PATH);
                RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"EventMessageFile", 0, REG_EXPAND_SZ, (BYTE*)path, (wcslen(path) + 1) * sizeof(WCHAR));
                
                DWORD types = EVENTLOG_ERROR_TYPE | EVENTLOG_WARNING_TYPE | EVENTLOG_INFORMATION_TYPE;
                RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"TypesSupported", 0, REG_DWORD, (BYTE*)&types, sizeof(DWORD));
                
                RegCloseKey(hKey);
            }
            RegisterVirtualPort();  // Register the port (without restarting spooler)
            LoadPortMappings();     // Load existing port mappings
            break;
        }
        case DLL_PROCESS_DETACH:
            PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop = true;
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.join();
            }
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.join();
            }
            break;
    }
    return TRUE;
}

# File: C:\Users\Slyphur\Documents\interceptor\README.md

Below is an extremely detailed step-by-step guide (a prompt or blueprint) explaining how to implement Approach A: a Full Custom Port Monitor (DLL) for Windows to intercept and modify spool data (e.g., ESC/POS) before it reaches a physical printer. This guide covers the architectural background, development environment setup, core monitor API functions, registry configuration, and advanced considerations like bidirectional I/O and spooler status reporting.

Overview
A port monitor in Windows is a dynamic-link library (DLL) that the printing subsystem (the spooler) loads to handle the final stage of sending data to a port. By writing your own monitor:

You gain access to the raw printer data stream.
You can modify or inspect it before sending it on to the real printer port (USB, COM, etc.).
You can intercept and respond to printer status queries so that the spooler and driver continue functioning normally.
The Windows spooler calls a set of standard entry points in your DLL (like InitializePrintMonitor2, OpenPort, WritePort, etc.). You will implement these functions in C++ using the Windows Driver Kit (WDK), then install and register your DLL as a custom monitor.

1. Development Environment Setup
Install the Windows Driver Kit (WDK)

Ensure it matches the target OS version (e.g., WDK for Windows 10, or the latest WDK if targeting Windows 11).
The WDK integrates with Visual Studio. Use a matching Visual Studio version recommended by the WDK.
Create a New Project

In Visual Studio, create a Dynamic-Link Library (DLL) project.
Set the platform to x64 if you are building for a 64-bit system.
Configure the project to use the WDK headers and libraries.
Include Required Headers

You’ll need standard Windows headers (<Windows.h>) and spooler-specific headers (e.g., winsplp.h, <winspool.h>).
For older spooler models, you may see references to monitor.h or localmon.h in the WDK samples.
Reference WDK Samples

Microsoft has provided sample port monitors in past WDKs (e.g., “localmon” or “serialmon”).
Studying them can clarify how the spooler expects your functions to be structured.
2. Basic Architecture of a Custom Port Monitor
2.1 Required (and Optional) Exported Functions
Historically (and depending on Windows version), you’ll implement one of the following initialization functions:

InitializePrintMonitor2

Modern approach (Windows Vista and later).
Returns a structure containing pointers to your monitor’s function implementations.
InitializePrintMonitor

Older approach.
Used on earlier versions of Windows.
Inside your implementation, you must provide pointers to (or implement directly) several monitor callbacks, typically:

OpenPort / OpenPortEx: Called when the spooler wants to open a port (e.g., your “MyVirtualPort:”).
ClosePort: Called when done with that port handle.
StartDocPort: Called at the start of a print job.
WritePort: The spooler calls this repeatedly to send data.
ReadPort: If your driver needs read-back or bidirectional comms.
EndDocPort: Called at the end of a print job.
GetPrinterDataFromPort: For advanced status retrieval from the device.
SetPortTimeOuts: If needed to configure timeouts for reads/writes.
2.2 Data Flow
Spooler calls OpenPort("MyVirtualPort:") → You return a handle/pointer to a context structure you manage.
Spooler calls StartDocPort(handle, jobId, pDocName, ...) → You initialize job-specific data if needed, possibly open a real device (e.g., \\.\USB001).
Spooler calls WritePort(handle, pData, cbData, &cbWritten) repeatedly → You receive chunks of ESC/POS or other data from the driver.
Here is where you can parse, modify, or log the data.
Then you call WriteFile (or similar) to send it to the real port.
Spooler calls EndDocPort(handle) → You finalize the job, flush any buffers, close the real device if you had it open.
Spooler calls ClosePort(handle) → Release any resources.
3. Step-by-Step Implementation
3.1 Define Your Monitor Structure (for InitializePrintMonitor2)
You’ll typically define a global structure like:

c
Copy
Edit
MONITOR2 MyMonitorFunctions = {
    sizeof(MONITOR2),
    MyOpenPort,
    MyOpenPortEx,
    MyStartDocPort,
    MyWritePort,
    MyReadPort,
    MyEndDocPort,
    MyClosePort,
    MyAddPort,
    MyAddPortEx,
    MyConfigurePort,
    MyDeletePort,
    MyGetPrinterDataFromPort,
    MySetPortTimeOuts,
    // ... possibly more depending on your target Windows version
};
Then implement each function (prefixed with My* or whichever naming scheme you choose).

3.2 DllMain
Your DLL must have a standard DllMain:

c
Copy
Edit
BOOL APIENTRY DllMain(HMODULE hModule, DWORD ul_reason_for_call, LPVOID lpReserved) {
    switch (ul_reason_for_call) {
    case DLL_PROCESS_ATTACH:
        // Perform initialization
        break;
    case DLL_PROCESS_DETACH:
        // Cleanup if needed
        break;
    }
    return TRUE;
}
3.3 InitializePrintMonitor2
c
Copy
Edit
PMONITOR2 WINAPI InitializePrintMonitor2(PMONITORINIT pMonitorInit, PHANDLE phMonitor) {
    // Optionally store the spooler callback interface or other data from pMonitorInit
    // e.g., pMonitorInit->cbSize, pMonitorInit->pMonitorReg, etc.
    
    // If you need to store any global state, allocate memory here using pMonitorInit->pfnAlloc
    // and return a handle to that state via phMonitor.

    // Finally, return a pointer to your MONITOR2 structure with function pointers.
    return &MyMonitorFunctions;
}
pMonitorInit is provided by the spooler, containing function pointers you can call for memory allocation, logging, registry access, etc.
phMonitor can be used if you have any global context to store.
3.4 Implementing Core Functions
Let’s detail the critical ones:

OpenPort

c
Copy
Edit
BOOL MyOpenPort(LPWSTR pName, PHANDLE pHandle) {
    // pName will be something like "MyVirtualPort:"
    // Create a context structure to hold port-specific info:
    PORT_CONTEXT *pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT *)AllocSplMem(sizeof(PORT_CONTEXT));
    if (!pPortCtx) return FALSE;

    // Initialize context (store port name, set up logs, etc.)
    wcscpy_s(pPortCtx->portName, MAX_PATH, pName);

    // Return pointer to context in *pHandle so spooler can reference it later.
    *pHandle = (HANDLE)pPortCtx;

    return TRUE;
}
You won’t actually open the physical device (USB or COM) here yet unless you want to. Usually, that’s deferred until the first document.
StartDocPort

c
Copy
Edit
BOOL MyStartDocPort(HANDLE hPort, LPWSTR pPrinterName, DWORD JobId, DWORD Level, LPBYTE pDocInfo) {
    PORT_CONTEXT *pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT *)hPort;
    // Typically parse pDocInfo if you need to log doc name, etc.
    
    // Optionally open the REAL device here, e.g.:
    // pPortCtx->hDevice = CreateFile(L"\\\\.\\USB001", ...);
    // or open network socket, etc.
    
    // If you need spooler job info, store it in pPortCtx.
    pPortCtx->jobId = JobId;
    return TRUE;
}
WritePort

c
Copy
Edit
BOOL MyWritePort(HANDLE hPort, LPBYTE pBuffer, DWORD cbBuf, LPDWORD pcbWritten) {
    PORT_CONTEXT *pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT *)hPort;

    // 1. Inspect or modify the data in pBuffer:
    //    e.g., parse ESC/POS commands to add/remove or log them.

    // 2. Forward the (potentially modified) data to the real printer:
    //    if (pPortCtx->hDevice) {
    //       WriteFile(pPortCtx->hDevice, pModifiedData, cbModified, pcbWritten, NULL);
    //    }

    // For now, let's assume you wrote everything successfully
    *pcbWritten = cbBuf;
    return TRUE;
}
This is where the core logic of intercepting/transforming ESC/POS commands occurs.
You might maintain an internal buffer that you parse for certain escape codes, then rewrite them.
EndDocPort

c
Copy
Edit
BOOL MyEndDocPort(HANDLE hPort) {
    PORT_CONTEXT *pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT *)hPort;
    
    // Finalize/flush/close any pending data.
    // e.g., if (pPortCtx->hDevice) {
    //    CloseHandle(pPortCtx->hDevice);
    //    pPortCtx->hDevice = NULL;
    // }
    
    return TRUE;
}
ClosePort

c
Copy
Edit
BOOL MyClosePort(HANDLE hPort) {
    PORT_CONTEXT *pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT *)hPort;
    
    // Release any allocated memory or resources
    FreeSplMem(pPortCtx);
    return TRUE;
}
3.5 Handling Status and Bidirectional I/O (Advanced)
ReadPort: If your printer sends back status bytes and the driver or spooler expects them, implement ReadPort. For example:
c
Copy
Edit
BOOL MyReadPort(HANDLE hPort, LPBYTE pBuffer, DWORD cbBuffer, LPDWORD pcbRead) {
    PORT_CONTEXT *pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT *)hPort;
    // e.g., ReadFile(pPortCtx->hDevice, pBuffer, cbBuffer, pcbRead, NULL);
    return TRUE;
}
GetPrinterDataFromPort: This function is sometimes used by spooler or the driver to retrieve specific data or status. If the Epson driver relies on it, you need to handle that:
c
Copy
Edit
DWORD MyGetPrinterDataFromPort(HANDLE hPort, DWORD controlID, LPWSTR pValueName, LPWSTR pInBuffer, DWORD cbInBuffer,
                               LPWSTR pOutBuffer, DWORD cbOutBuffer, DWORD dwFlags, LPDWORD pcbReturned) {
    // Implement logic to respond with status info, etc.
    return ERROR_SUCCESS;
}
Bidirectional printers (especially receipt printers) often require real-time status responses (paper out, cover open, etc.). Carefully implement these functions so the spooler sees valid status data.

4. Registry Configuration
To register your custom port monitor with Windows:

Copy Your DLL to the appropriate location:

For 64-bit Windows, typically:
makefile
Copy
Edit
C:\Windows\System32\spool\drivers\x64\3\MyPortMonitor.dll
Or sometimes simply C:\Windows\System32\MyPortMonitor.dll (depending on spooler’s search path).
Create Registry Keys:

Location: HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Print\Monitors\MyPortMonitor
String value: Driver = MyPortMonitor.dll
It should look like:

ini
Copy
Edit
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Print\Monitors\MyPortMonitor]
"Driver"="MyPortMonitor.dll"
Restart the Print Spooler:

net stop spooler
net start spooler
Check the spooler logs or event logs for any error loading your monitor.

5. Creating and Using the Port
Once installed, you need to:

Add a New Port in the Printer UI

Go to Devices and Printers → Right-click your printer → Printer Properties → Ports → Add Port... → Select MyPortMonitor from the list → Create a port named, e.g., "MyVirtualPort:".
Alternatively, you can programmatically call AddPort, or you can implement MyAddPort in your DLL so it appears in the UI.
Assign the Printer to Use Your Port

In the Printer Properties → Ports tab, check the box for "MyVirtualPort:" so that the spooler sends the job to your monitor instead of a USB or network port.
Test Print

Print a test page or a real receipt.
Your WritePort function should receive the spool data, letting you examine or modify it before passing it to the real device.
6. Debugging and Logging
Debug Logging

Use standard Win32 APIs like OutputDebugString or the spooler’s callback pMonitorInit->pfnLog to record debug messages.
Write logs to a file on disk to confirm you’re receiving data in WritePort.
Attaching a Debugger

The spooler (spoolsv.exe) runs as a service, so you can attach Visual Studio’s debugger (or WinDbg) to that process.
Symbolic debugging can be tricky but is often necessary if you run into crashes or unexpected spooler behavior.
Common Errors

Missing or incorrect registry entries.
Dll not found (ensure your path is correct).
32-bit vs. 64-bit mismatch.
Not implementing a required function for the spooler version you’re on.
7. Advanced Considerations
Memory Management

Typically, for spooler-provided memory management, you’ll use the spooler’s function pointers from pMonitorInit->pfnAlloc, pMonitorInit->pfnFree, etc., to stay consistent with spooler memory usage.
Performance

Receipt printing typically involves small, quick jobs. Still, ensure WritePort doesn’t become a bottleneck. If you do heavy parsing, consider buffering or keep it efficient.
Multi-Port Support

If your monitor will handle multiple “MyVirtualPort:”, “MyVirtualPort2:” etc., you might store an array or list of PORT_CONTEXT structures. Each call to OpenPort returns a new context.
User Interaction

Typically, port monitors run under the spooler’s service context (session 0). Showing UI can be problematic in modern Windows. If you need user prompts, you may have to rely on a separate helper application or custom approach.
64-Bit vs. 32-Bit

On a 64-bit OS, the spooler is typically a 64-bit process. You must build your DLL as 64-bit.
If you also need 32-bit support for some reason (legacy subsystem), you’d produce a separate 32-bit build. Usually only the 64-bit is needed on modern systems.
Digital Signing

In some environments, you may need to digitally sign your driver package or monitor. Unlike kernel drivers, a port monitor is user-mode, so code signing isn’t always strictly required. But some corporate environments might require it.
Returning Correct Status

If the printer is out of paper or jammed, the driver/spooler might call ReadPort or GetPrinterDataFromPort to check status bits. Ensure you handle that logic if the user expects correct spooler status.
8. Summary / Final Words
Implementing a full custom port monitor is the most robust method to intercept, modify, and forward print data in Windows. Here’s the concise bullet of what you do:

Create a DLL using the WDK.
Export InitializePrintMonitor2 (or the older InitializePrintMonitor), returning a table of function pointers (MONITOR2 structure).
Implement at least OpenPort, ClosePort, StartDocPort, EndDocPort, and WritePort.
Install your DLL and register it in the Registry under HKLM\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Print\Monitors\YourMonitorName.
Restart the spooler, create a new port using your monitor, and assign that port to your existing printer queue.
Intercept the data in WritePort—log, parse, or alter the ESC/POS commands—then forward to the real hardware port.
Handle any bidirectional needs in ReadPort or GetPrinterDataFromPort so your driver remains fully functional.
Result: You have an in-spooler “man-in-the-middle,” letting you reliably intercept and transform ESC/POS or any other raw data without breaking the normal Windows printing pipeline.

HANDLE CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(LPCWSTR pipeName, DWORD openMode, DWORD pipeMode, PSECURITY_ATTRIBUTES pSA) {
    HANDLE hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    int retryCount = 0;
    const int maxRetries = 3;
    DWORD lastError = 0;

    while (retryCount < maxRetries && hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        WriteToEventLog(L"Attempting to create named pipe: ", pipeName);
        
        hPipe = CreateNamedPipeW(
            pipeName,
            openMode,
            pipeMode,
            PIPE_UNLIMITED_INSTANCES,
            BUFFER_SIZE,
            BUFFER_SIZE,
            0,
            pSA
        );

        if (hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            lastError = GetLastError();
            std::wstring errorMsg = L"Failed to create pipe. Error code: " + std::to_wstring(lastError);
            if (lastError == ERROR_PIPE_BUSY) {
                errorMsg += L" (Pipe is busy)";
            } else if (lastError == ERROR_ACCESS_DENIED) {
                errorMsg += L" (Access denied)";
            }
            WriteToEventLog(errorMsg.c_str());
            retryCount++;
            if (retryCount < maxRetries) {
                Sleep(1000); // Wait before retry
            }
        } else {
            // Verify pipe is accessible
            DWORD flags = 0;
            BOOL result = GetNamedPipeInfo(hPipe, &flags, NULL, NULL, NULL);
            if (!result) {
                lastError = GetLastError();
                WriteToEventLog(L"Pipe created but not accessible. Error: ", std::to_wstring(lastError).c_str());
            } else {
                WriteToEventLog(L"Successfully created and verified pipe: ", pipeName);
            }
        }
    }

    if (hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        WriteToEventLog(L"Failed to create pipe after all retries");
    }

    return hPipe;
}

BOOL APIENTRY DllMain(HMODULE hModule, DWORD ul_reason_for_call, LPVOID lpReserved) {
    switch (ul_reason_for_call) {
        case DLL_PROCESS_ATTACH: {
            // Register event source
            HKEY hKey;
            DWORD disposition;
            if (RegCreateKeyExW(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE,
                L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Services\\EventLog\\Application\\PrinterInterceptor",
                0, NULL, REG_OPTION_NON_VOLATILE, KEY_SET_VALUE, NULL, &hKey, &disposition) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                
                wchar_t path[MAX_PATH];
                GetModuleFileNameW(hModule, path, MAX_PATH);
                RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"EventMessageFile", 0, REG_SZ, (BYTE*)path, (wcslen(path) + 1) * sizeof(WCHAR));
                
                DWORD types = EVENTLOG_ERROR_TYPE | EVENTLOG_WARNING_TYPE | EVENTLOG_INFORMATION_TYPE;
                RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"TypesSupported", 0, REG_DWORD, (BYTE*)&types, sizeof(DWORD));
                
                RegCloseKey(hKey);
            }

            RegisterVirtualPort();  // Register the port (without restarting spooler)
            LoadPortMappings();     // Load existing port mappings
            break;
        }
        case DLL_PROCESS_DETACH:
            PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop = true;
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.join();
            }
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.join();
            }
            break;
    }
    return TRUE;
}

void WriteToEventLog(const wchar_t* message1, const wchar_t* message2) {
    HANDLE hEventLog = RegisterEventSourceW(NULL, L"PrinterInterceptor");
    if (hEventLog) {
        std::wstring fullMessage = message1;
        if (message2) {
            fullMessage += message2;
        }
        const wchar_t* messages[] = { fullMessage.c_str() };
        ReportEventW(hEventLog, EVENTLOG_INFORMATION_TYPE, 0, 0, NULL, 1, 0, messages, NULL);
        DeregisterEventSource(hEventLog);
    }
}

void WriteToEventLog(const char* message) {
    size_t size = strlen(message) + 1;
    wchar_t* wmessage = new wchar_t[size];
    size_t convertedChars = 0;
    mbstowcs_s(&convertedChars, wmessage, size, message, _TRUNCATE);
    WriteToEventLog(wmessage);
    delete[] wmessage;
}

# File: C:\Users\Slyphur\Documents\interceptor\src\routes\+page.svelte

<script lang="ts">
  import { onMount } from 'svelte';
  import { invoke } from '@tauri-apps/api/core';

  let ports: string[] = [];
  let selectedOutputPort: string = "";
  let textToInject: string = "";

  // On component mount, enumerate available ports
  onMount(async () => {
    try {
      ports = await invoke("get_ports");
      if (ports.length > 0) {
        selectedOutputPort = ports[0];
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Error enumerating ports:", err);
      //alert("Could not enumerate ports, see console for details.");
      alert(err);
    }
  });

  async function setPort() {
    try {
      await invoke("set_active_port", { realPort: selectedOutputPort });
      alert(`Redirecting "SplitPrinterInterceptor" → ${selectedOutputPort}`);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      alert(`Error setting port: ${err}`);
    }
  }

  async function injectText() {
    try {
      await invoke("inject_print_command", { text: textToInject });
      alert("Injected text into spooler!");
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      alert(`Error injecting text: ${err}`);
    }
  }
</script>

<h1>Printer Ports</h1>
<div>
  <label>Select Output Port:</label>
  <select bind:value={selectedOutputPort}>
    {#each ports as p}
      <option value={p}>{p}</option>
    {/each}
  </select>
</div>

<button on:click={setPort}>
  Set Output Port
</button>

<hr />

<div>
  <label>Inject Print Data:</label>
  <textarea rows="3" bind:value={textToInject}></textarea>
</div>
<button on:click={injectText}>
  Inject Print Data
</button>


# File: C:\Users\Slyphur\Documents\interceptor\src-interceptor\Logger.h

#pragma once

#include <Windows.h>
#include <string>

void WriteToLog(const wchar_t* message, const wchar_t* additionalInfo = nullptr) {
    try {
        // Get the Windows directory
        wchar_t winDir[MAX_PATH];
        GetWindowsDirectoryW(winDir, MAX_PATH);

        // Create the log file path
        std::wstring logPath = std::wstring(winDir) + L"\\Temp\\PrinterInterceptor.log";

        // Get current timestamp
        SYSTEMTIME st;
        GetLocalTime(&st);
        wchar_t timestamp[64];
        swprintf_s(timestamp, L"%04d-%02d-%02d %02d:%02d:%02d.%03d",
            st.wYear, st.wMonth, st.wDay,
            st.wHour, st.wMinute, st.wSecond, st.wMilliseconds);

        // Format the log message
        std::wstring logMessage = std::wstring(timestamp) + L" - " + message;
        if (additionalInfo) {
            logMessage += L": " + std::wstring(additionalInfo);
        }
        logMessage += L"\r\n";

        // Open the file in append mode
        HANDLE hFile = CreateFileW(
            logPath.c_str(),
            FILE_APPEND_DATA,
            FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE,
            NULL,
            OPEN_ALWAYS,
            FILE_ATTRIBUTE_NORMAL,
            NULL
        );

        if (hFile != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            // Write UTF-16 BOM if this is a new file
            if (GetLastError() != ERROR_ALREADY_EXISTS) {
                WORD bom = 0xFEFF;
                DWORD written;
                WriteFile(hFile, &bom, sizeof(bom), &written, NULL);
            }

            // Write the message
            DWORD written;
            WriteFile(hFile, logMessage.c_str(), (DWORD)(logMessage.length() * sizeof(wchar_t)), &written, NULL);
            CloseHandle(hFile);
        }

        // Also write to debug output
        OutputDebugStringW(logMessage.c_str());

    } catch (...) {
        // If logging fails, at least try to output to debug
        OutputDebugStringW(L"Error writing to log file\n");
        OutputDebugStringW(message);
        if (additionalInfo) {
            OutputDebugStringW(L": ");
            OutputDebugStringW(additionalInfo);
        }
        OutputDebugStringW(L"\n");
    }
} 

# File: C:\Users\Slyphur\Documents\interceptor\src-interceptor\PrinterInterceptor.cpp

// PrinterInterceptor.cpp

#include <Windows.h>
#include <winreg.h>
#include <winspool.h>
#include <winsplp.h>
#include <fstream>
#include <string>
#include <sstream>
#include <iomanip>
#include <ctime>
#include <vector>
#include <thread>
#include <atomic>
#include <queue>
#include <mutex>
#include <map>
#include <aclapi.h>  // For security functions
#include <sddl.h>    // For security descriptor functions
#include "Logger.h"  // For WriteToLog function

// Constants for registry access
#define REG_PORT_KEY L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Control\\Print\\Monitors\\PrinterInterceptor\\Ports"
#define REG_CONFIG_KEY L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Control\\Print\\Monitors\\PrinterInterceptor\\Config"
#ifdef PIPE_NAME
#undef PIPE_NAME
#endif
#define PIPE_NAME L"\\\\.\\pipe\\PrinterInterceptorPipe"
#ifdef PORT_COMMAND_PIPE
#undef PORT_COMMAND_PIPE
#endif
#define PORT_COMMAND_PIPE L"\\\\.\\pipe\\PrinterInterceptorPortPipe"
#define PIPE_BUFFER_SIZE 4096

// Add these new structures
struct PortMapping {
    std::wstring virtualPort;
    std::wstring realPort;
};

struct PrintCommand {
    std::vector<BYTE> data;
    DWORD timestamp;
};

// Port context structure to maintain state
struct PORT_CONTEXT {
    WCHAR portName[MAX_PATH];      // Name of our port
    WCHAR realPortName[MAX_PATH];  // Name of the real printer port
    HANDLE hRealPort;              // Handle to the real printer port
    DWORD jobId;                   // Current job ID
    std::wofstream* logFile;       // Log file for this port
    std::vector<BYTE> buffer;      // Buffer for accumulating print data
    
    // Static members for pipe communication
    static HANDLE hPipe;
    static HANDLE hPortPipe;
    static std::thread pipeThread;
    static std::thread portPipeThread;
    static std::queue<PrintCommand> commandQueue;
    static std::mutex queueMutex;
    static std::atomic<bool> shouldStop;
    static std::map<std::wstring, std::wstring> portMappings;
    static std::mutex portMappingsMutex;

    PORT_CONTEXT() : hRealPort(INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE), jobId(0), logFile(nullptr) {
        portName[0] = L'\0';
        realPortName[0] = L'\0';
    }

    ~PORT_CONTEXT() {
        if (logFile) {
            logFile->close();
            delete logFile;
        }
        if (hRealPort != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            CloseHandle(hRealPort);
        }
    }
};

// Initialize static members
HANDLE PORT_CONTEXT::hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
HANDLE PORT_CONTEXT::hPortPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
std::thread PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread;
std::thread PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread;
std::queue<PrintCommand> PORT_CONTEXT::commandQueue;
std::mutex PORT_CONTEXT::queueMutex;
std::atomic<bool> PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop(false);
std::map<std::wstring, std::wstring> PORT_CONTEXT::portMappings;
std::mutex PORT_CONTEXT::portMappingsMutex;

// Common ESC/POS commands
const BYTE ESC = 0x1B;
const BYTE LF = 0x0A;
const BYTE CR = 0x0D;

// Add these new global variables at the top of the file after the includes
static HANDLE g_hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
static HANDLE g_hPortPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;

// Add CreateNamedPipeWithRetry function implementation
HANDLE CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(LPCWSTR pipeName, DWORD openMode, DWORD pipeMode, int maxRetries) {
    std::wstring message;
    
    // Initialize security descriptor components
    PSID pEveryoneSID = NULL;
    PACL pACL = NULL;
    PSECURITY_DESCRIPTOR pSD = NULL;
    SECURITY_ATTRIBUTES sa;
    
    try {
        // Create and initialize the Everyone SID
        SID_IDENTIFIER_AUTHORITY SIDAuthWorld = SECURITY_WORLD_SID_AUTHORITY;
        if (!AllocateAndInitializeSid(&SIDAuthWorld, 1, SECURITY_WORLD_RID,
            0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, &pEveryoneSID)) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to initialize Everyone SID");
        }

        // Calculate the ACL size needed
        DWORD dwAclSize = sizeof(ACL) + sizeof(ACCESS_ALLOWED_ACE) + GetLengthSid(pEveryoneSID) - sizeof(DWORD);
        
        // Allocate memory for the ACL
        pACL = (PACL)LocalAlloc(LPTR, dwAclSize);
        if (pACL == NULL) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to allocate memory for ACL");
        }

        // Initialize the ACL
        if (!InitializeAcl(pACL, dwAclSize, ACL_REVISION)) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to initialize ACL");
        }

        // Add the Everyone ACE to the ACL with full access
        if (!AddAccessAllowedAce(pACL, ACL_REVISION, GENERIC_ALL | FILE_ALL_ACCESS, pEveryoneSID)) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to add ACE to ACL");
        }

        // Create and initialize the security descriptor
        pSD = (PSECURITY_DESCRIPTOR)LocalAlloc(LPTR, SECURITY_DESCRIPTOR_MIN_LENGTH);
        if (pSD == NULL) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to allocate security descriptor");
        }

        if (!InitializeSecurityDescriptor(pSD, SECURITY_DESCRIPTOR_REVISION)) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to initialize security descriptor");
        }

        // Set the ACL in the security descriptor
        if (!SetSecurityDescriptorDacl(pSD, TRUE, pACL, FALSE)) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Failed to set security descriptor DACL");
        }

        // Set up the security attributes
        sa.nLength = sizeof(SECURITY_ATTRIBUTES);
        sa.lpSecurityDescriptor = pSD;
        sa.bInheritHandle = FALSE;

        // Create the pipe with retries
        for (int retry = 1; retry <= maxRetries; retry++) {
            message = L"Attempting to create named pipe: " + std::wstring(pipeName) + L", Retry: " + std::to_wstring(retry);
            WriteToLog(message.c_str());

            HANDLE hPipe = CreateNamedPipeW(
                pipeName,
                openMode,
                pipeMode,
                PIPE_UNLIMITED_INSTANCES,
                4096,
                4096,
                0,
                &sa
            );

            if (hPipe != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
                message = L"Successfully created pipe: " + std::wstring(pipeName);
                WriteToLog(message.c_str());

                // Test pipe accessibility
                HANDLE hTest = CreateFileW(
                    pipeName,
                    GENERIC_READ | GENERIC_WRITE,
                    0,
                    &sa,
                    OPEN_EXISTING,
                    0,
                    NULL
                );

                if (hTest != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
                    CloseHandle(hTest);
                    // Clean up security resources
                    if (pEveryoneSID) FreeSid(pEveryoneSID);
                    if (pACL) LocalFree(pACL);
                    if (pSD) LocalFree(pSD);
                    return hPipe;
                }

                DWORD error = GetLastError();
                message = L"Pipe created but not accessible. Error: " + std::to_wstring(error);
                WriteToLog(message.c_str());
                CloseHandle(hPipe);
            }

            if (retry < maxRetries) {
                Sleep(1000);
            }
        }

        throw std::runtime_error("Failed to create pipe after all retries");
    }
    catch (const std::exception& e) {
        message = L"Error in CreateNamedPipeWithRetry: " + std::wstring(e.what(), e.what() + strlen(e.what()));
        WriteToLog(message.c_str());
    }

    // Clean up security resources
    if (pEveryoneSID) FreeSid(pEveryoneSID);
    if (pACL) LocalFree(pACL);
    if (pSD) LocalFree(pSD);
    
    return INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
}

// Helper function to get current timestamp
static std::wstring GetTimestamp() {
    auto now = std::time(nullptr);
    auto tm = *std::localtime(&now);
    std::wstringstream wss;
    wss << std::put_time(&tm, L"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S");
    return wss.str();
}

// Helper function to format data as hex dump
static std::wstring HexDump(LPBYTE data, DWORD size) {
    std::wstringstream wss;
    for (DWORD i = 0; i < size; i++) {
        if (i > 0 && i % 16 == 0) wss << L"\n";
        wss << std::hex << std::setw(2) << std::setfill(L'0') << static_cast<int>(data[i]) << L" ";
    }
    return wss.str();
}

// Helper function to check if a buffer ends with a complete print command
static bool IsCompletePrintCommand(const std::vector<BYTE>& buffer) {
    // Look for common end-of-print sequences
    if (buffer.empty()) return false;

    // Check for common end sequences like Form Feed (0x0C), multiple Line Feeds, etc.
    if (buffer.back() == 0x0C) return true;  // Form Feed
    
    // Check for multiple line feeds at the end
    if (buffer.size() >= 2 && 
        buffer[buffer.size()-1] == LF &&
        buffer[buffer.size()-2] == LF) {
        return true;
    }

    // Check for ESC @ (printer reset/initialize)
    if (buffer.size() >= 2 &&
        buffer[buffer.size()-2] == ESC &&
        buffer[buffer.size()-1] == '@') {
        return true;
    }

    return false;
}

// Helper function to create ESC/POS command sequence for text
static std::vector<BYTE> CreateTextCommand(const std::string& text) {
    std::vector<BYTE> cmd;
    
    // Initialize printer
    cmd.push_back(ESC);
    cmd.push_back('@');
    
    // Set text alignment to left
    cmd.push_back(ESC);
    cmd.push_back('a');
    cmd.push_back(0);
    
    // Add the text
    cmd.insert(cmd.end(), text.begin(), text.end());
    
    // Add line feeds
    cmd.push_back(CR);
    cmd.push_back(LF);
    cmd.push_back(LF);
    
    return cmd;
}

// Add these new functions before MyEnumPorts
void PipeServerThread() {
    WriteToLog(L"PipeServerThread: Starting...");
    
    while (!PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop) {
        WriteToLog(L"PipeServerThread: Creating new pipe instance...");
        
        // Create the named pipe with proper security attributes
        DWORD openMode = PIPE_ACCESS_INBOUND;
        DWORD pipeMode = PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT;
        
        wchar_t msg[256];
        swprintf_s(msg, L"PipeServerThread: Creating pipe with openMode=0x%x, pipeMode=0x%x", openMode, pipeMode);
        WriteToLog(msg);

        if (g_hPipe != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            CloseHandle(g_hPipe);
            g_hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
        }

        g_hPipe = CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(
            PIPE_NAME,
            openMode,
            pipeMode,
            5
        );

        if (g_hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            WriteToLog(L"PipeServerThread: Failed to create pipe after all retries");
            Sleep(1000);
            continue;
        }

        WriteToLog(L"PipeServerThread: Waiting for client connection...");
        
        BOOL connected = ConnectNamedPipe(g_hPipe, NULL);
        if (!connected) {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            if (error != ERROR_PIPE_CONNECTED) {
                swprintf_s(msg, L"PipeServerThread: ConnectNamedPipe failed. Error: %lu", error);
                WriteToLog(msg);
                CloseHandle(g_hPipe);
                g_hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
                continue;
            }
        }

        WriteToLog(L"PipeServerThread: Client connected. Processing data...");
        
        std::vector<BYTE> buffer(PIPE_BUFFER_SIZE);
        DWORD bytesRead;

        if (ReadFile(g_hPipe, buffer.data(), PIPE_BUFFER_SIZE, &bytesRead, NULL)) {
            if (bytesRead > 0) {
                wchar_t msg[256];
                swprintf_s(msg, L"PipeServerThread: Read %lu bytes from pipe", bytesRead);
                WriteToLog(msg);
                
                buffer.resize(bytesRead);
                PrintCommand cmd;
                cmd.data = buffer;
                cmd.timestamp = GetTickCount();

                // Add to queue
                {
                    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(PORT_CONTEXT::queueMutex);
                    PORT_CONTEXT::commandQueue.push(cmd);
                    WriteToLog(L"PipeServerThread: Added command to queue");
                }
            }
        } else {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            wchar_t errorMsg[256];
            swprintf_s(errorMsg, L"PipeServerThread: ReadFile failed. Error: %lu", error);
            WriteToLog(errorMsg);
        }

        DisconnectNamedPipe(g_hPipe);
        CloseHandle(g_hPipe);
        g_hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }
    
    if (g_hPipe != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        CloseHandle(g_hPipe);
        g_hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }
    
    WriteToLog(L"PipeServerThread: Exiting...");
}

// Add these new functions for registry and port management
void LoadPortMappings() {
    HKEY hKey;
    if (RegOpenKeyExW(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, REG_PORT_KEY, 0, KEY_READ, &hKey) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
        WCHAR subKeyName[MAX_PATH];
        DWORD subKeyNameSize = MAX_PATH;
        DWORD index = 0;

        while (RegEnumKeyExW(hKey, index++, subKeyName, &subKeyNameSize, NULL, NULL, NULL, NULL) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
            HKEY hSubKey;
            if (RegOpenKeyExW(hKey, subKeyName, 0, KEY_READ, &hSubKey) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                WCHAR realPortName[MAX_PATH] = { 0 };
                DWORD dataSize = sizeof(realPortName);
                
                if (RegQueryValueExW(hSubKey, L"RealPortName", NULL, NULL, (LPBYTE)realPortName, &dataSize) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(PORT_CONTEXT::portMappingsMutex);
                    PORT_CONTEXT::portMappings[subKeyName] = realPortName;
                }
                
                RegCloseKey(hSubKey);
            }
            subKeyNameSize = MAX_PATH;
        }
        
        RegCloseKey(hKey);
    }
}

void PortConfigThread() {
    WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Starting...");
    
    while (!PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop) {
        WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Creating new pipe instance...");
        
        if (g_hPortPipe != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            CloseHandle(g_hPortPipe);
            g_hPortPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
        }

        g_hPortPipe = CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(
            PORT_COMMAND_PIPE,
            PIPE_ACCESS_INBOUND,
            PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT,
            5
        );

        if (g_hPortPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Failed to create pipe after all retries");
            Sleep(1000);
            continue;
        }

        WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Waiting for client connection...");
        
        BOOL connected = ConnectNamedPipe(g_hPortPipe, NULL);
        if (!connected) {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            if (error != ERROR_PIPE_CONNECTED) {
                wchar_t errorMsg[256];
                swprintf_s(errorMsg, L"PortConfigThread: ConnectNamedPipe failed. Error: %lu", error);
                WriteToLog(errorMsg);
                CloseHandle(g_hPortPipe);
                g_hPortPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
                continue;
            }
        }

        WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Client connected. Processing data...");
        
        WCHAR buffer[PIPE_BUFFER_SIZE];
        DWORD bytesRead;

        if (ReadFile(g_hPortPipe, buffer, PIPE_BUFFER_SIZE * sizeof(WCHAR), &bytesRead, NULL)) {
            if (bytesRead > 0) {
                wchar_t msg[256];
                swprintf_s(msg, L"PortConfigThread: Read %lu bytes from pipe", bytesRead);
                WriteToLog(msg);
                
                std::wstring realPort(buffer, bytesRead / sizeof(WCHAR));

                WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Updating port mappings...");
                {
                    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(PORT_CONTEXT::portMappingsMutex);
                    PORT_CONTEXT::portMappings[L"SplitPrinterInterceptor"] = realPort;
                }

                // Update registry so this mapping persists
                WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Updating registry...");
                HKEY hKey;
                std::wstring keyPath = L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Control\\Print\\Ports\\SplitPrinterInterceptor";
                LONG result = RegOpenKeyExW(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, keyPath.c_str(), 0, KEY_WRITE, &hKey);
                if (result == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                    result = RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"RealPortName", 0, REG_SZ, 
                        (BYTE*)realPort.c_str(), (realPort.length() + 1) * sizeof(WCHAR));
                    if (result != ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                        wchar_t errorMsg[256];
                        swprintf_s(errorMsg, L"PortConfigThread: Failed to set registry value. Error: %lu", result);
                        WriteToLog(errorMsg);
                    }
                    RegCloseKey(hKey);
                } else {
                    wchar_t errorMsg[256];
                    swprintf_s(errorMsg, L"PortConfigThread: Failed to open registry key. Error: %lu", result);
                    WriteToLog(errorMsg);
                }
            }
        } else {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            wchar_t errorMsg[256];
            swprintf_s(errorMsg, L"PortConfigThread: ReadFile failed. Error: %lu", error);
            WriteToLog(errorMsg);
        }

        DisconnectNamedPipe(g_hPortPipe);
        CloseHandle(g_hPortPipe);
        g_hPortPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }
    
    if (g_hPortPipe != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        CloseHandle(g_hPortPipe);
        g_hPortPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }
    
    WriteToLog(L"PortConfigThread: Exiting...");
}

// Modify DllMain to handle both threads
void RegisterVirtualPort() {
    HKEY hKey;
    std::wstring keyPath = L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Control\\Print\\Ports\\SplitPrinterInterceptor";

    if (RegCreateKeyExW(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, keyPath.c_str(), 0, NULL, 0, KEY_WRITE, NULL, &hKey, NULL) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
        // Simply register the port monitor without restarting the spooler.
        RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"Monitor", 0, REG_SZ, (BYTE*)L"PrinterInterceptor", (wcslen(L"PrinterInterceptor") + 1) * sizeof(WCHAR));
        RegCloseKey(hKey);
    }
}

BOOL APIENTRY DllMain(HMODULE hModule, DWORD ul_reason_for_call, LPVOID lpReserved) {
    switch (ul_reason_for_call) {
        case DLL_PROCESS_ATTACH:
            RegisterVirtualPort();  // Register the port (without restarting spooler)
            LoadPortMappings();     // Load existing port mappings
            break;
        case DLL_PROCESS_DETACH:
            PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop = true;
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.join();
            }
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.join();
            }
            break;
    }
    return TRUE;
}

// Implementation of required functions
BOOL WINAPI MyEnumPorts(HANDLE hMonitor, LPWSTR pName, DWORD Level, LPBYTE pPorts, DWORD cbBuf, LPDWORD pcbNeeded, LPDWORD pcReturned) {
    *pcbNeeded = 0;
    *pcReturned = 0;
    return TRUE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MyOpenPort(HANDLE hMonitor, LPWSTR pName, PHANDLE pHandle) {
    PORT_CONTEXT* pPortCtx = new PORT_CONTEXT();
    if (!pPortCtx) return FALSE;

    // Store our port name
    wcscpy_s(pPortCtx->portName, MAX_PATH, pName);

    // Get the real port name from our mappings
    {
        std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(PORT_CONTEXT::portMappingsMutex);
        auto it = PORT_CONTEXT::portMappings.find(pName);
        if (it != PORT_CONTEXT::portMappings.end()) {
            wcscpy_s(pPortCtx->realPortName, MAX_PATH, it->second.c_str());
        } else {
            // Fallback to default behavior: strip "INTERCEPT:" prefix
            if (wcslen(pName) > 10) {
                wcscpy_s(pPortCtx->realPortName, MAX_PATH, pName + 9);
            }
        }
    }

    // Create log file
    std::wstring logPath = L"C:\\PrinterLogs\\";
    CreateDirectoryW(L"C:\\PrinterLogs", NULL);
    
    std::wstring timestamp = GetTimestamp();
    std::wstring logName = logPath + L"printer_" + timestamp + L".log";
    pPortCtx->logFile = new std::wofstream(logName, std::ios::out | std::ios::binary);

    if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Port Monitor Log - " << timestamp << L"\n";
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Port: " << pPortCtx->portName << L"\n";
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Real Port: " << pPortCtx->realPortName << L"\n\n";
        pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
    }

    *pHandle = (HANDLE)pPortCtx;
    return TRUE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MyStartDocPort(HANDLE hPort, LPWSTR pPrinterName, DWORD JobId, DWORD Level, LPBYTE pDocInfo) {
    PORT_CONTEXT* pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT*)hPort;
    if (!pPortCtx) return FALSE;

    pPortCtx->jobId = JobId;

    // Open the real port
    if (pPortCtx->realPortName[0] != L'\0') {
        pPortCtx->hRealPort = CreateFileW(pPortCtx->realPortName,
            GENERIC_READ | GENERIC_WRITE,
            0,  // No sharing
            NULL,
            OPEN_EXISTING,
            FILE_ATTRIBUTE_NORMAL,
            NULL);
    }

    if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"\nStarting Job " << JobId << L" on printer " << pPrinterName << L"\n";
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Timestamp: " << GetTimestamp() << L"\n\n";
        pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
    }

    return TRUE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MyWritePort(HANDLE hPort, LPBYTE pBuffer, DWORD cbBuf, LPDWORD pcbWritten) {
    PORT_CONTEXT* pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT*)hPort;
    if (!pPortCtx) return FALSE;

    // Log the original data
    if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"\nWrite operation at " << GetTimestamp() << L"\n";
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Original data size: " << cbBuf << L" bytes\n";
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Original data (hex):\n" << HexDump(pBuffer, cbBuf) << L"\n\n";
        pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
    }

    // Add the data to our buffer
    pPortCtx->buffer.insert(pPortCtx->buffer.end(), pBuffer, pBuffer + cbBuf);

    // Check if we have a complete print command
    if (IsCompletePrintCommand(pPortCtx->buffer)) {
        std::vector<BYTE> additionalText;

        // Check for dynamic commands in the queue
        {
            std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(PORT_CONTEXT::queueMutex);
            if (!PORT_CONTEXT::commandQueue.empty()) {
                additionalText = PORT_CONTEXT::commandQueue.front().data;
                PORT_CONTEXT::commandQueue.pop();
            } else {
                // Fallback to default text if no dynamic commands are available
                additionalText = CreateTextCommand("The light brown fox jumps over the lazy river");
            }
        }

        // Log the modification
        if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
            *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Adding additional text to print data\n";
            *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Additional data size: " << additionalText.size() << L" bytes\n";
            *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Additional data (hex):\n" << HexDump(additionalText.data(), additionalText.size()) << L"\n\n";
        }

        // Forward the original data to real port if available
        if (pPortCtx->hRealPort != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            DWORD bytesWritten = 0;
            
            // Write the original data
            BOOL success = WriteFile(pPortCtx->hRealPort, pPortCtx->buffer.data(), pPortCtx->buffer.size(), &bytesWritten, NULL);
            if (!success) {
                if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
                    *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Error writing original data to real port: " << GetLastError() << L"\n";
                    pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
                }
                return FALSE;
            }

            // Write our additional text
            success = WriteFile(pPortCtx->hRealPort, additionalText.data(), additionalText.size(), &bytesWritten, NULL);
            if (!success) {
                if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
                    *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Error writing additional text to real port: " << GetLastError() << L"\n";
                    pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
                }
                return FALSE;
            }

            *pcbWritten = cbBuf;  // Report original size as written
        } else {
            // If no real port, pretend we wrote everything
            *pcbWritten = cbBuf;
        }

        // Clear the buffer for the next print job
        pPortCtx->buffer.clear();
    } else {
        // Not a complete command yet, just report the bytes as written
        *pcbWritten = cbBuf;
    }

    return TRUE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MyReadPort(HANDLE hPort, LPBYTE pBuffer, DWORD cbBuffer, LPDWORD pcbRead) {
    PORT_CONTEXT* pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT*)hPort;
    if (!pPortCtx) return FALSE;

    // Try to read from real port if available
    if (pPortCtx->hRealPort != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        BOOL success = ReadFile(pPortCtx->hRealPort, pBuffer, cbBuffer, pcbRead, NULL);
        if (!success) {
            if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
                *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Error reading from real port: " << GetLastError() << L"\n";
                pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
            }
            return FALSE;
        }

        // Log what we read
        if (pPortCtx->logFile && *pcbRead > 0) {
            *pPortCtx->logFile << L"\nRead operation at " << GetTimestamp() << L"\n";
            *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Data size: " << *pcbRead << L" bytes\n";
            *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Data (hex):\n" << HexDump(pBuffer, *pcbRead) << L"\n\n";
            pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
        }
    } else {
        *pcbRead = 0;
    }

    return TRUE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MyEndDocPort(HANDLE hPort) {
    PORT_CONTEXT* pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT*)hPort;
    if (!pPortCtx) return FALSE;

    if (pPortCtx->logFile) {
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"\nEnding Job " << pPortCtx->jobId << L"\n";
        *pPortCtx->logFile << L"Timestamp: " << GetTimestamp() << L"\n\n";
        pPortCtx->logFile->flush();
    }

    // Close real port if open
    if (pPortCtx->hRealPort != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        CloseHandle(pPortCtx->hRealPort);
        pPortCtx->hRealPort = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
    }

    return TRUE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MyClosePort(HANDLE hPort) {
    PORT_CONTEXT* pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT*)hPort;
    if (pPortCtx) {
        delete pPortCtx;
    }
    return TRUE;
}

    return FALSE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MyGetPrinterDataFromPort(HANDLE hPort, DWORD ControlID, LPWSTR pValueName, 
    LPWSTR lpInBuffer, DWORD cbInBuffer, LPWSTR lpOutBuffer, DWORD cbOutBuffer, LPDWORD lpcbReturned) {
    *lpcbReturned = 0;
    return FALSE;
}

BOOL WINAPI MySetPortTimeOuts(HANDLE hPort, LPCOMMTIMEOUTS lpCTO, DWORD reserved) {
    PORT_CONTEXT* pPortCtx = (PORT_CONTEXT*)hPort;
    if (!pPortCtx || pPortCtx->hRealPort == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) return FALSE;

    // Forward timeout settings to real port
    return SetCommTimeouts(pPortCtx->hRealPort, lpCTO);
}

// Export the initialization function
PMONITOR2 WINAPI InitializePrintMonitor2(PMONITORINIT pMonitorInit, PHANDLE phMonitor) {
    *phMonitor = NULL;
    return &MonitorFunctions;
} 

extern "C" __declspec(dllexport) BOOL StartInterceptorThreads() {
    try {
        WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Starting...");
        
        // Stop any existing threads first
        if (PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.joinable() || PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.joinable()) {
            WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Stopping existing threads...");
            PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop = true;
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.join();
            }
            if (PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.joinable()) {
                PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.join();
            }
        }

        // Reset the stop flag
        PORT_CONTEXT::shouldStop = false;

        // Create initial pipes
        WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Creating initial pipes...");
        
        PORT_CONTEXT::hPipe = CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(
            PIPE_NAME,
            PIPE_ACCESS_INBOUND,
            PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT,
            5
        );

        if (PORT_CONTEXT::hPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Failed to create main pipe");
            return FALSE;
        }

        PORT_CONTEXT::hPortPipe = CreateNamedPipeWithRetry(
            PORT_COMMAND_PIPE,
            PIPE_ACCESS_INBOUND,
            PIPE_TYPE_MESSAGE | PIPE_READMODE_MESSAGE | PIPE_WAIT,
            5
        );

        if (PORT_CONTEXT::hPortPipe == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            CloseHandle(PORT_CONTEXT::hPipe);
            PORT_CONTEXT::hPipe = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE;
            WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Failed to create port pipe");
            return FALSE;
        }

        // Start the pipe server thread
        WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Starting pipe server thread...");
        PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread = std::thread(PipeServerThread);

        // Start the port configuration thread
        WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Starting port configuration thread...");
        PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread = std::thread(PortConfigThread);

        // Wait a moment to ensure threads are running
        Sleep(2000);

        // Verify pipes are still accessible
        WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Verifying pipes after thread start...");
        HANDLE hTest = CreateFileW(
            PIPE_NAME,
            GENERIC_READ | GENERIC_WRITE,
            0,
            NULL,
            OPEN_EXISTING,
            0,
            NULL
        );

        if (hTest == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            wchar_t errorMsg[256];
            swprintf_s(errorMsg, L"Main pipe not accessible after thread start. Error: %lu", error);
            WriteToLog(errorMsg);
        } else {
            CloseHandle(hTest);
            WriteToLog(L"Main pipe verified accessible after thread start");
        }

        hTest = CreateFileW(
            PORT_COMMAND_PIPE,
            GENERIC_READ | GENERIC_WRITE,
            0,
            NULL,
            OPEN_EXISTING,
            0,
            NULL
        );

        if (hTest == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
            DWORD error = GetLastError();
            wchar_t errorMsg[256];
            swprintf_s(errorMsg, L"Port pipe not accessible after thread start. Error: %lu", error);
            WriteToLog(errorMsg);
        } else {
            CloseHandle(hTest);
            WriteToLog(L"Port pipe verified accessible after thread start");
        }

        // Only detach if we got this far without errors
        if (PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.joinable()) {
            WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Detaching pipe server thread...");
            PORT_CONTEXT::pipeThread.detach();
        }
        if (PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.joinable()) {
            WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Detaching port configuration thread...");
            PORT_CONTEXT::portPipeThread.detach();
        }

        WriteToLog(L"StartInterceptorThreads: Completed successfully");
        return TRUE;
    }
    catch (const std::exception& e) {
        wchar_t errorMsg[256];
        size_t convertedChars = 0;
        mbstowcs_s(&convertedChars, errorMsg, e.what(), _TRUNCATE);
        WriteToLog(L"Error in StartInterceptorThreads", errorMsg);
        return FALSE;
    }
}

// Add this exported function at the end of the file, after DllMain
extern "C" __declspec(dllexport) BOOL InstallVirtualPort() {
    try {
        RegisterVirtualPort();
        return TRUE;
    } catch (...) {
        return FALSE;
    }
}

    "Capability": {
      "description": "A grouping and boundary mechanism developers can use to isolate access to the IPC layer.\n\nIt controls application windows fine grained access to the Tauri core, application, or plugin commands. If a window is not matching any capability then it has no access to the IPC layer at all.\n\nThis can be done to create groups of windows, based on their required system access, which can reduce impact of frontend vulnerabilities in less privileged windows. Windows can be added to a capability by exact name (e.g. `main-window`) or glob patterns like `*` or `admin-*`. A Window can have none, one, or multiple associated capabilities.\n\n## Example\n\n```json { \"identifier\": \"main-user-files-write\", \"description\": \"This capability allows the `main` window on macOS and Windows access to `filesystem` write related commands and `dialog` commands to enable programatic access to files selected by the user.\", \"windows\": [ \"main\" ], \"permissions\": [ \"core:default\", \"dialog:open\", { \"identifier\": \"fs:allow-write-text-file\", \"allow\": [{ \"path\": \"$HOME/test.txt\" }] }, ], \"platforms\": [\"macOS\",\"windows\"] } ```",

    "Capability": {
      "description": "A grouping and boundary mechanism developers can use to isolate access to the IPC layer.\n\nIt controls application windows fine grained access to the Tauri core, application, or plugin commands. If a window is not matching any capability then it has no access to the IPC layer at all.\n\nThis can be done to create groups of windows, based on their required system access, which can reduce impact of frontend vulnerabilities in less privileged windows. Windows can be added to a capability by exact name (e.g. `main-window`) or glob patterns like `*` or `admin-*`. A Window can have none, one, or multiple associated capabilities.\n\n## Example\n\n```json { \"identifier\": \"main-user-files-write\", \"description\": \"This capability allows the `main` window on macOS and Windows access to `filesystem` write related commands and `dialog` commands to enable programatic access to files selected by the user.\", \"windows\": [ \"main\" ], \"permissions\": [ \"core:default\", \"dialog:open\", { \"identifier\": \"fs:allow-write-text-file\", \"allow\": [{ \"path\": \"$HOME/test.txt\" }] }, ], \"platforms\": [\"macOS\",\"windows\"] } ```",
